Administering Oath to a Jew or Christian: The Hanafi Formula and Its Proof
Procedure for oaths to Jews and Christians by mentioning their prophets' scriptures

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi formula for administering an oath to a Jew and to a Christian, and explain the dalil from the Prophet's practice with Ibn Suriya.

Core Idea
A Jew is sworn by Allah who revealed the Torah, a Christian by Allah who revealed the Gospel.

When a qadi needs to administer an oath to a non-Muslim litigant, the Hanafi school specifies a unique formula that mentions the scripture revealed to that person's prophet. This lesson unpacks the exact wording from the matn, the reasoning behind it, and the decisive proof from a famous incident in the Prophet's life. Understanding this ruling helps you appreciate how the school tailors judicial procedure to the beliefs of the witnesses for maximum deterrence.

Guided Path
1
Identify the ruling
Read the first part of the passage carefully. State exactly what formula the qadi uses for a Jew and for a Christian. Note the words 'qala' (he said) indicates the matn author's ruling.
The formula is: 'By Allah who revealed the Torah to Moses' for a Jew, and 'By Allah who revealed the Gospel to Jesus' for a Christian.
2
Understand the rationale (taghlith)
The passage gives two reasons: (1) the Prophet's practice, and (2) the psychological effect on the person. Jews revere Moses and the Torah; Christians revere Jesus and the Gospel. Mentioning these makes the oath more binding and deters perjury.
Taghlith = emphasis by mentioning something sacred to the person.
3
Examine the primary proof: the Ibn Suriya incident
The commentary narrates the story: a Jew had his face blackened for adultery. The Prophet called their scholar Ibn Suriya and adjured him by Allah who revealed the Torah, asking about the real penalty. Ibn Suriya admitted stoning was in the Torah. The Prophet then ordered stoning. This shows the Prophet himself used this formula.
This is a Sunnah ahad hadith; its meaning is clear and binding.
4
Analyse the second proof: deterrence
The second proof is based on the principle that people are more careful when something they hold sacred is invoked. Since Jews believe in Moses and Christians in Jesus, quoting their scripture adds weight to the oath.
This is a rational (qiyas) extension of the practice, but the primary proof remains the hadith.
5
Note the practical application
The Hanafi position is that this formula is wajib (obligatory). The Shafi'i school generally allows any customary formula, but the Hanafis insist on this specific wording due to the clear precedent. The mufta bihi is the formula as stated.
No intra-Hanafi ikhtilaf is recorded.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
یہودی اور نصرانی سے قسم لینے کا طریقہ
قال ويستحلف اليهودى بالله الذى انزل التوراة على موسى عليه السلام والنصراني بالله الذي انزل الانجيل على عيسى عليه السلام لقوله صلى الله عليه واله وسلم لابن صوريا الاعور انشدك الله الذی انزل التوراة على موسى ان حكم الزنا فى كتابكم هذا ولان اليهودى يعتقد نبوة موسى والنصراني نبوة عيسى عليه السلام فيغلظ على كل واحد منهما بـ ا بذكر المنزل على نبيا
ترجمہ یہودی سے قسم لی جائے کہ اس اللہ کی قسم جس نے موسی پر تورات اتاری ہے اور نصرانی سے اس اللہ کی قسم جس نے عیسی پر انجیل اتاری ہے کیونکہ آنحضرت صلى الله عليه وسلم نے ابن صور یا اعور سے کہا میں تجھ کو اس اللہ کی قسم دلاتا ہوں جس نے موسی پر تو رات اتاری کہ زنا کا حکم تمہاری کتاب میں یہی ہے اور اس لئے کہ یہودی موسیٰ کی نبوت کا معتقد ہے اور نصرانی عیسی کی نبوت کا اعتقاد رکھتا ہے پس قاضی ان میں سے ہر ایک پر اس کتاب کا ذکر کر کے تغلیظ کرے جو اسکے نبی پر اتاری ہے۔
تشریح شیخ ابوالحسن قدوری نے کہا کہ قاضی یہودی سے قسم اس طرح کھلائے باللہ الذی انزل التوراة على موسیٰ اس خدا کی قسم جس نے موسیٰ پر تو رات اتاری اور نصرانی سے اس طرح قسم کھلائے بالله الذی انزل الانجیل علی عیسیٰ اس خدا کی قسم جس نے عیسی پر انجیل اتاری ہے۔
دلیل یہ ہے کہ ایک بار آنحضرت صلى الله عليه وسلم اس یہودی کے پاس سے گذرے جس کا منہ زنا کی سزاء میں کالا کئے ہوئے تھے آپ نے یہودی کو بلا کر دریافت کیا کہ کیا تمہاری کتاب میں زنا کی یہی سزاء ہے سب نے کہا۔ ہاں۔ اس کے بعد آپ صلى الله عليه وسلم نے یہودی کے ایک عالم عبد اللہ بن صور یا کو بلایا اور کہا کہ تم کو اس خدا کی قسم جس نے موسیٰ پر تو رات اتاری ہے کیا تمہاری کتاب میں حد زنا یہی ہے ابن صوریا نے کہا نہیں بلکہ ہماری کتاب میں حد زنار حجم ہے اور دیکھو محمد اگر آپ مجھ کو قسم نہ کھلاتے تو میں بھی آپ کو اس کی خبر نہ دیتا۔ ابن صوریا نے کہا کہ واقعہ اصل یہ ہے کہ جب شرفاء اور غیر شرفاء کے درمیان تقسیم کی کہ اگر کوئی شریف آدمی اس کا مرتکب ہوگا تو اس کا صرف منہ کالا کیا جائے گا اور کسی غیر شریف نے یہ حرکت کی تو اس کو کوڑے لگائے جائیں گے اور رجم کو ہم نے بالکل ترک کر دیا حالانکہ تورات میں رحم ہی کا حکم ہے آپ صلى الله عليه وسلم نے پورا واقعہ سن کر اس زانی کو رجم کرنے کا حکم فرمایا اور معصومانہ اور عاشقانہ انداز میں یوں فرمایا اللهم انى اول من احیا امرك اذا ما تو وہ اے اللہ میں پہلا آدمی ہوں جس نے تیرا حکم زندہ کیا حالانکہ یہود اس کو دفن کر چکے تھے۔ اس واقعہ سے بھی معلوم ہوا کہ یہود اور نصاری سے مذکورہ الفاظ کے ساتھ قسم لی جائے گی۔ دوسری دلیل یہ ہے کہ یہود حضرت موسیٰ کی نبوت پر اعتقادر کھتے ہیں اور نصاریٰ حضرت عیسی کی نبوت پر اعتقادر کھتے ہیں پس جھوٹی قسم سے پر ہیز کرانے کے لئے قاضی ان میں سے ہر ایک اس کتاب کو ذکر کر کے تغلیظ کرے گا جو کتاب ان کے نبی پر اتاری گئی ہے۔
Method of taking oath from a Jew or Christian. He said: And a Jew is sworn by Allah who revealed the Torah to Moses (peace be upon him), and a Christian by Allah who revealed the Gospel to Jesus (peace be upon him) because the Prophet (PBUH) said to Ibn Suriya the One-Eyed: 'I adjure you by Allah who revealed the Torah to Moses, is the ruling of adultery in your book this?' and because the Jew believes in the prophethood of Moses and the Christian believes in the prophethood of Jesus (peace be upon them). So each is made emphatic by mentioning the revealed book to his prophet. Translation: A Jew should be sworn: 'By Allah who revealed the Torah to Moses' and a Christian: 'By Allah who revealed the Gospel to Jesus' because the Prophet (PBUH) said to Ibn Suriya the One-Eyed: 'I adjure you by Allah who revealed the Torah to Moses, is the ruling of adultery in your book this?' and because the Jew believes in Messianic prophethood and the Christian believes in Jesus' prophethood. So the qadi emphasizes for each by mentioning the book revealed to his prophet. Commentary: Shaykh Abu al-Hasan al-Quduri said: The qadi swears a Jew with the words 'By Allah who revealed the Torah to Moses' and a Christian with 'By Allah who revealed the Gospel to Jesus.' The proof: Once the Prophet (PBUH) passed by a Jew whose face had been blackened as a punishment for adultery. He called the Jews and asked if this was the punishment in their book. They all said yes. Then he called the Jew's scholar Abdullah ibn Suriya and said, 'I adjure you by Allah who revealed the Torah to Moses, is the hadd of adultery this in your book?' Ibn Suriya said no, rather the hadd in our book is stoning, and look, Muhammad, if you had not made me swear, I would not have informed you. He then explained that they had set different punishments for nobles and commoners and had abandoned stoning. The Prophet heard the full story and ordered the adulterer to be stoned, saying, 'O Allah, I am the first to revive your command when they had buried it.' From this incident, it is learned that Jews and Christians are sworn with these words. The second proof: Jews believe in Musa's prophethood and Christians in Isa's, so to deter false oaths, the qadi emphasizes for each by mentioning the book revealed to their prophet.
Source pages p. 344

Commentary
This passage provides the ruling and proof for how a qadi should administer an oath to a Jew or Christian. The ruling from the matn is that the qadi says: 'By Allah who revealed the Torah to Moses' for a Jew, and 'By Allah who revealed the Gospel to Jesus' for a Christian. The primary evidence is a famous incident from the Prophet's life involving Ibn Suriya, a Jewish scholar. The Prophet adjured him by Allah and the Torah, and Ibn Suriya admitted the truth under the weight of that oath. The second proof is that Jews and Christians revere their prophets, so mentioning the scripture sent to their prophet serves as an effective deterrent against perjury. The commentary expands on the story to illustrate the practice.

Key Terms
انشدك (anshaduka): I adjure you / I ask you by Allah – a form of oath administration.
تغلیظ (taghlith): Emphasis in the oath by mentioning specifically revered beings or attributes.
يستحلف (yustahlaf): He is sworn / the oath is administered to him.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
What is the primary proof for swearing a Jew 'by Allah who revealed the Torah to Moses'?
A) A general hadith about swearing
B) The incident with Ibn Suriya where the Prophet used that formula
C) The Quranic verse about the Torah
D) Consensus of the Companions

Key Takeaway
The Hanafi school prescribes specific oath formulas for Jews and Christians based on their scriptures, derived from the Prophet's practice with Ibn Suriya.
